myne empire haue folowed sticked haue bene twyse ouerthrowen field twyse enforced flye away fidelitie constancy maketh thinke remayne still kyng traitours fugitiues reigne cyties thought worthy suche vngrateful shal due comendacios extolle sterres though determined still haue fled whereuto harte neuer agreed yet haue conceyued suche truste vertue man hode purpose passe myne enemy howe long shall banisshed within myne dominion straunge forein prince flye within boundes myne owne kingdome may hasarding battaill either recouer haue loste el dye honest death except peraduenture semeth better submit enemy thensample mazens mithrenes receiue peticion dominion one nacion wherin iuge alexander rather folowe thinclinacyon glorie hys wrath let god neuer graunte may lye man powre eyther take vrkesomnes enemy neither proud porte stately lokes euery man ryght hand shall giue vnto hym self either reuenge end thes euils nothing stand long one stay selfe ensample alteracion fortune without cause loke better change worst fall god wyll neds againste v warres lauful honeste yet cannot taken v may alway manfully honestly dye require make intercession honor predecessor suche fame glory within asya departed minde geueth shortly shal restore vnto againe countrey bactria yet vntouched indian saeans apointement many people many armes many thousandes horseman foteme haue force redines renue warre yt muche greater force remaineth yt cosumed like beastes wilfully runne distruction necessary ye pertie men courage rather dispise death hate life oftentymes werines trauayll towardes driuen take little regarde selues vertue leaueth nothing vnprouided death beynge ende thynges sufficient god yt lyke sluggardes therefore shal go vnto bactria next refuge let v time sake make bessus kynges obstinat mynde attempted worcke hym religion whiche greater force declared hym goddes determinacion whiche signified great perill ensue passed ryuer said vnderstande thyng aristaunder told hym comming pauilion perceiued beastes intrailes alexa der vpon wordes wonderfully troubled anger shame sawe secretes religion brought light thought haue kept secrete self therfore caused erigius go aside aristander called vnto beheld face said seme rather priuate man king seing commaunded make sacrifice thou hast declared significatio therof erigius thy report knoweth priuities pertaining sure iudge feare deuised interpretacion himselfe therfore let heare thyne mouth yu hast found intrailes thintent thou shalt deny thou hast spoken arista der therupo amased loked pale able answere one word feare length feare made holde peace pricked forwardes speake lest prolonging kinges expectacion might prouoke wrath answered said qd enterprise great daunger difficultie yet yt attept shuld vaine nothing haue perceiued sciece trouble much loue beare towardes cosider infirmitie momet co sisteth owne persone fearing shuld able endure thinges fortune disposed geue vnto alexander hard speake maner willed haue confidence felicitie fortune graunted glory greater thinges therupo dismissed afterwardes king debating suche cosulted meanes shuld passe riuer arista der came amonges affirming found intrailes contrary yt likely signes good successe yt euer sawe shewig great cause reioyse feare immediatly hereupon receiued newes yt muche appaired continuall felicitie wont haue procedinges menedemus sent hath bene said besiege spitamenes auctour bactrians rebellion vnderstode enemy coming auoidig enclosed within walles trusting besides take aduau tage macedos laid imbushemet entrappe wood thei shuld passe apt ye purpose laid dahas whose custome cary two armed men vpon one horse whence vsed leape course reason swiftnes footemen little inferior vnto horseme troubled greatly ordre horseman fight spitamenes gaue ordre whe enemy shuld enter wood enuirone side whiche perfourmed according appointmet menedemus seing self enclosed al part equall nombre vnto enemy resisted greate crieng souldiers remayned hope intrapt maner making slaughter vpon enemy receiue co fort honest death menedemus rid vpon strog horse charging oft time vpon enemy wherby brake ordre made great slaughter till tyme laid parteshispydes receiued many woundes fainted want bloud exhorted hispides one frendes leape vpon horse escape away worde swounded fel ground horse hispides might haue got away lost fred determined die taking care spend life losse enemy wherfore put spoores horse ranne amonges fought notably lengthe slayne reste sawe thys ouerthrowe losse capitaine recouered hill spitamenes besiege thinking subdue want vitaill slaine battaill two footemen iii hundred horseman whiche misadueture alexander great policy kept secret commaunding parted field vnder payne death publyshe matter abrode could beare lenger countenaunce contrary harte went alone vnto pauilion whiche set purpose vpo riuers side waked night deuising selfe best doe diuers time lifted vp tent behold fire enemy campe therby coniecture matter required spoken king could say reason infirmitie souldiers went matter suche good cherefulnes mind within thre day thei finished xiim boates whe al thinges prepared redines passage came xx copasse europe thou goest asia fro asia passe europe muste come passe thou ouercome mankynde thou muste kepe warre woodes snowes riuers wilde beastes art thou ignorant tree growe till great plucked vp rote momente foole doth couet frute considereth height tree wheron growith take hed lest while thou doost labour attaine vnto toppe thou falleste wyth boous thou doest embrace lion hath bene tyme foode smalle byrd ruste doth consume iron nothing sure daungier hys inferior haue wyth neuer touched thy countrey lawfull v liue wast woodes ignoraunt thou arte whence thou commest neither subiect man desire rule ouer creature bicause ye shal ignorant thestate nacion haue certayne giftes proper vnto v yoke ox plough speare bowe bowle thyngs vse wyth frendes enemy giue vnto frendes frutes gotten gloryfie art come parsecuter theues arte robber nacions thou comeste amonges thou haste taken lydia possessed siria enioyed perce haste bactrians vnder thy power thou dost visite indie streachest furth thy rauenowes hand vnto cattel dost thou couet rich cause pore thou art first al men haboundance hast prepared thy self honger thou haste gredely thou doste couet ye thing thou haste dost thou remebre loge thou hast stiked bactria while thou goest subdue sogdians begin rebel thus warre doth growe vnto thy victorie thou neuer great force aboue yet ther none endure gouerned straungers passe nowe tanais thou shalt parceyue bredth beareth yet thou shalt neuer ouertake scithias whose pouertie swyfter thy army cariing ye spoile many nacios attaine whe thou shalt thinke v farre thou shalt see v within thy campe like swiftnes folowe fle away heare desertes beskorned greake prouerbes couet rather desertes place vnhabited city plentiful countres therefore hold thou thy fortune fast slipper cannot kept agaynst hir wyll folowe thou counsell yt good specially whilles tyme doth serue put bridle thy felicitye thou shalt gouerne better saye fortune without feete hath hand winges whe putteth furth hand wil suffre hir winges touched thou god geue benefites vnto mortal men take away commodity haue alredy thou man considre alwaye thine owne estate folishe remembre thynges cause forget thy selfe suche warre thou makest thy enemy peace thou maist make thy veray frendes firme fredship amogest equal seme equall haue yet made trial ther force take hede thou take thy frendes thou doest fronte battaile put macedos terrour troublyng vnwonted crye onely horse naturally feare also amased men disturbed order muche thei whiche little thought selues victorers loked aboute whiche waye flee saue theim selues whiche thinge alexander perceiued sente elephantes agrians tharians men light armed apter skyrmish farre fight hande hand gaue elephantes gouernours muche doo sore afflicted wyth multitude dartes arrowes bestowed amonges phalanx came constantly forwardes againste feare suche pressed ouer forwarde fyghtynge wyth elephantes procured manifest destruction beynge trampeled death wyth fete example ouer hastye aduenturynge selues moste terrible sight elephantes wyth longe trunkes whiche called probostides toke menne armoure grounde deliuered vp gouernours battaile prolonged doubtfully tyll daye farre spente souldiours sometime fliyng elephantes sometime pursuing vntil certaine kynde weapon called copida whyche croked lyke sithes prepared purpose cut elephantes vpon legges macedon right aptly deuised onely feare death also feare newe kinde torment death caused leaue nothynge vnproued finally elephantes weried woundes violente struglynge raste gouernoures earth tare piece put fear hurtfull enemy driue battayle like shepe porus beynge forsaken parte hys men ceassed caste dartes wherof plentye prepared vpon hys elephant amonges flocked aboute hym wherby woundyng manye reason laye open euerye mannes blowe layed partes tyll hadde receiued nine woundes behynde throughe whiche bledde muche power cast feblenes fell hys handes elephante also whyche didde ryde vpon pricked forwardes wyth furye made great disturbaunce amonges macedon vntyll hys gouernoure seynge kynge faynte let fall hys dartes almost past hys remembraunce sturred beast flee awaye alexander folowed myght horse thrust wyth manye woundes fel downe deade vnder wherfore while aboute chaunge take caste farre behinde meane season taxiles brother sent alexander vnto porus began exhorte abstinate proue extremitye rather yelde selfe vnto victorer notwithstandyng strength nere past bloude fayled yet sturred vp knowen voyce saied knewe brother taxiles traytoure hys king countrey word toke dart whiche chaunce fallen awaye threwe taxyles brother passed throughe middes hys breste vnto hys backe hauynge shewed last profe manhode fled agayne faster elephant many woundes receiued fainted like sort stayed turned fotemen towards enemy folowed time alexader come nere vnderstandyng wilfulnes porus willed none spared made resistaunce wherupon euery man threw dartes porus suche fotemen stode defece wherwith length oppressed began fal elephant indian wyiche gouernoure thinkyng porus desiered haue lighted caused beast hys accustomed maner bende towarde earth whyche submittynge
